Abstract: Sign language translation (SLT) remains constrained by limited paired sign-video/text corpora and heavy-tailed target vocabularies. We study target-side augmentation in which GPT-4o generates controlled paraphrase variants of reference sentences while the sign input remains unchanged. A Signformer-style pose-based Transformer is trained under a two-stage schedule: pre-training on the augmented corpus followed by fine-tuning on the original references.
  We evaluate on three datasets spanning complementary challenges: PHOENIX14T (German Sign Language), with moderate lexical diversity; GSL (Greek Sign Language), with highly ontrolled, repetitive recordings; and LSA-T (Argentinian Sign Language), with severe long-tail sparsity. On PHOENIX14T, augmentation improves BLEU-4 from 9.56 to 10.33. The near-saturated GSL baseline and extremely sparse LSA-T setting reveal the limits of the approach. To our knowledge, this is the first study to apply LLM-generated target-side araphrases and LLM-as-a-Judge evaluation to SLT. The semantic evaluation reveals gains in fidelity that lexical overlap metrics understate.

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) largely follow the text-only LLM trajectory, excelling on English benchmarks but sharply degrading on low-resource languages, where neither large-scale image-text corpora nor culturally grounded evaluations exist. We translate established English VLM training and evaluation corpora into Romanian, applying machine translation to textual annotations and to in-image text, preserving visual grounding while adapting the textual content. Using this data, we train and ablate a series of VLMs to isolate the contribution of (i) vision backbones of varying scale and pretraining, (ii) language backbones from multilingual to Romanian-adapted LLMs, and (iii) OCR-style image-text data. ### [204] [The Sword, Shield, and Achilles' Heel: Characterizing the Linguistic Inductive Bias of Large Language Models for Spatial Reasoning in Navigation Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31404)
*Xudong Zhang,Jian Yang,Shengkai Wang,Jiangpeng Tian,Shaowen Chen,Xian Wei,Ke Li,Xiong You*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种双重干预框架，系统分析了大模型导航中语言结构和上下文要素对模型推理能力的影响，强调合理设计文本空间表示对于提升导航准确性的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的大模型导航系统通常将空间信息转化为文本输入，但文本的语言结构与背景特征选择常被视为普通工程细节，未深入探究其对模型表现的关键影响。本文旨在揭示不同文本空间表示和上下文处理方式对LLM导航计划的实际作用机制和潜在偏好。

Method: 提出双重干预框架：一是对文本空间表示的语言格式和压缩程度进行干预，分析不同表示何时促进或阻碍导航规划；二是对上下文要素的组合及冲突进行干预，明确LLM在处理空间线索时的优势和弱点。在多种空间推理任务和不同规模的LLM上进行实证对比评估。

Result: 发现拓扑信息是一致且强韧的导航支撑，语言格式的作用随模型规模、任务难度和压缩程度变化而存在双重影响，语义信息则最易出错，错误线索会导致导航全面失败。不同模型与任务需求下，导航性能对空间信息表达有高度敏感性。

Conclusion: LLM导航任务中，文本空间表示应优先保留拓扑清晰度、根据模型能力调整压缩程度、准确处理语义信息，切忌统一或随意设计空间表达。合理表达结构能够显著提升导航准确性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM)-based navigation systems commonly construct explicit spatial representations (e.g., topological graphs, semantic raster maps) and translate them into textual descriptions as LLMs' inputs. However, the linguistic structures of such text-based spatial representations and the choices of contextual features (e.g., topology, geometry) they contain are often treated as neutral engineering decisions rather than key factors that shape LLMs' behavior. To fill the gap, we propose a dual-interventional framework that disentangles linguistic structures from different contextual cues to evaluate the linguistic inductive bias of LLMs for navigation planning. In the framework, representation intervention varies the linguistic format and the degree of linguistic compression, clarifying when linguistic representations support or inhibit navigation planning. Context intervention, combined with contextual feature combination and conflict probing, explicitly clarifies the preferences and weaknesses of LLMs when processing different contextual cues. Experiments across diverse spatial reasoning tasks and multiple model scales reveal a consistent pattern: topological information is a sturdy shield and the backbone of robust planning; linguistic format is a double-edged sword whose effect depends on model size, task demands, and the compression level; and semantic information is a fatal Achilles' heel -- incorrect semantic cues can systematically derail the planning process. Overall, our study shows that effective text-based spatial representations in LLM-based navigation should preserve topological integrity, calibrate representational compression to model capacity, and ensure semantic correctness, rather than simply adopting a single representation. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/jonesdong150/LLM-Navigation-Inductive-Bias.

</details>


### [205] [Skill Availability and Presentation Granularity in Large-Language-Model Agents: A Controlled SkillsBench Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31408)
*Xiaonan Xu,Wenjing Wu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了技能文档在推理时为大语言模型（LLM）代理的任务表现带来的影响，尤其关注技能知识的呈现粒度对下游任务成功率的作用。结果显示，有无技能知识的差异带来了显著性能提升，而粒度的不同影响较小且不确定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管技能文档有助于大模型在实际任务中的推理和成功，但尚不清楚其内容粒度如何影响模型的表现。因此，作者希望明确技能文档的粒度（如高/低抽象度，带/不带示例）是否对任务结果有显著作用。

Method: 作者构建了平衡任务领域的SkillsBench子集，涵盖30项任务，针对两种主流模型（GPT-5.5和DeepSeek V4-Flash），设置六种技能条件，并在每对任务-条件-模型配置下进行五次实验。通过比较不同粒度与有/无技能知识等条件下的表现，评估其对任务成功率的影响。

Result: 在有技能文档时，GPT-5.5的平均通过率提升26.7~36个百分点，DeepSeek V4-Flash提升18~26个百分点。不同粒度（高/低抽象度、是否带示例）引入的表现差异很小，置信区间包含0，且不同模型间略有不同。稳健性检验同样支持主要结论。

Conclusion: 技能文档的提供显著提升了大模型在推理任务中的表现。但在本实验条件下，技能知识的呈现粒度（细/粗、是否带示例）对任务成功率影响较小且结果不确定，具体效果还依赖于模型类型。

Abstract: Skill documents provide procedural knowledge to large-language-model agents at inference time. This article studies whether the presentation granularity of controlled skill knowledge changes downstream task success. The experiment uses a pinned SkillsBench version, a 30-task domain-balanced subset validated by official oracle runs, two reasoning-enabled model configurations, six skill conditions, and five trials per task-condition-model cell. Skill availability is the clearest empirical signal. Relative to no skill, skill conditions increase task-mean pass rate by 26.7 to 36.0 percentage points for GPT-5.5 and by 18.0 to 26.0 percentage points for DeepSeek V4-Flash. The final data contain 1,800 rows, with 900 rows for each model. The task is the inference unit. Five trials are aggregated within each task-condition-model cell before paired contrasts are estimated over 30 tasks. The primary presentation contrasts are smaller and uncertain. Low-abstraction guidance differs from high-abstraction guidance by +0.7 percentage points for GPT-5.5 and -6.7 percentage points for DeepSeek V4-Flash, with both 95% bootstrap confidence intervals crossing zero. Adding one worked example to medium-abstraction guidance differs from the no-example variant by +0.7 and +1.3 percentage points. Mean-reward robustness checks preserve the same substantive conclusion. In this controlled subset, skill availability is associated with higher success than no skill, while the tested presentation-granularity changes yield small, uncertain, and model-dependent effects.

### [206] [Neuro-symbolic Syntactic Parsing: Shaping a Neural Network with the CYK Algorithm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31421)
*Fabio Massimo Zanzotto,Federico Ranaldi,Giorgio Satta*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经网络难以直接执行复杂符号算法，尤其是在语法解析、结构化数据等任务上往往表现不佳。作者希望探索用可训练神经结构直接模拟算法执行流程，提高模型在这些领域的能力。

Method: 作者以CYK算法（处理Chomsky范式上下文无关文法的解析算法）为例，将其流程映射为可微分、可训练的矩阵-向量运算，设计了专用的循环神经网络结构CYKNN。

Conclusion: 将算法直接注入神经网络结构是一种可行的新思路，为神经-符号融合方法拓展了新方向，尤其在结构化符号任务上具有潜力。

Abstract: In this paper, we show the possibility of a direct injection of algorithms into neural network architecture. We focus on a complex algorithm, that is, Cocke-Youger-Kasami (CYK) for parsing context-free grammars in Chomsky Normal Form and we propose CYKNN, a simple recurrent neural network architecture for encoding the CYK algorithm in trainable matrix-vector multiplications.We experimented with a very simple grammar with 4 variations showing that our approach outperforms existing LLMs with more than 20B parameters with an in-context learning setting and smaller LLMs of the Qwen family fine-tuned with LoRA. Our attempt paves the way to a different approach to neuro-symbolic methodologies.

### [207] [DOA: Training-Free Decoder-Only Attention Policy for Long-Form Simultaneous Translation with SpeechLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31432)
*Sara Papi,Luisa Bentivogli*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种名为Decoder-Only Attention (DOA)的无训练策略，可直接在现成的SpeechLLMs架构下实现高质量低延迟的长篇同步语音翻译，无需对模型进行重新训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有同步语音翻译方法主要依赖于基于注意力的编码器-解码器模型，通过交叉注意力获得明确的对齐信号。然而，最新的SpeechLLMs采用仅解码器的自注意力结构，缺乏显式的对齐信号，其解码器自注意力是否足以提供同步翻译所需的稳定对齐指导成为待解决的重要问题。同时，现有策略多依赖训练适配或启发式wait-k政策，且未在长文本下充分验证。

Method: 作者提出了一种名为Decoder-Only Attention (DOA)的训练无关策略，通过从解码器自注意力中推导代理对齐信号，使得无需额外训练即可支持现成SpeechLLMs上的低延迟长文本同步翻译。

Result: 在Phi4-Multimodal和Qwen3-Omni两个模型上的实验结果表明，DOA策略能有效提供对齐信号，支持流式决策，带来接近离线解码质量的低延迟长文本同步语音翻译。

Conclusion: DOA无需对SpeechLLMs进行重训练，即可实现高质量的长文本同步语音翻译，将同步策略从训练和启发式转向基于自注意力，增强了SpeechLLMs在实际流式应用中的适用性。

Abstract: Simultaneous speech-to-text translation (SimulST) generates translations while speech is still unfolding, requiring a streaming policy that decides when to read and when to write. State-of-the-art approaches rely on attention-based encoder-decoder models where cross-attention provides explicit alignment signals. In contrast, Speech Large Language Models (SpeechLLMs) are decoder-only architectures relying solely on self-attention. This raises a central question: whether decoder self-attention contains sufficiently stable alignment signals to guide the streaming policy. Moreover, existing approaches typically rely on training-based adaptations or heuristic wait-$k$ policies and have not been validated in long-form settings. To fill these gaps, we propose Decoder-Only Attention (DOA), a training-free policy that enables long-form simultaneous translation with off-the-shelf SpeechLLMs by deriving a proxy alignment from self-attention. Experiments on Phi4-Multimodal and Qwen3-Omni show that DOA provides an effective alignment signal for supporting streaming decisions, enabling low-latency long-form SimulST with quality close to offline decoding without retraining.

</details>


### [208] [SCOPE: Self-Play via Co-Evolving Policies for Open-Ended Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31433)
*Wai-Chung Kwan,Aryo Pradipta Gema,Joshua Ong Jun Leang,Pasquale Minervini*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种无需外部数据的自博弈（self-play）方法SCOPE，通过模型协同进化提升大模型在开放式任务上的能力，显著优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自博弈方法大多依赖可规则检查的问题，无法直接推广到开放式任务，需要人工编写提示或依赖更强大模型的评判，限制了自博弈的通用性和实用性。

Method: SCOPE框架包括两个互相协作的策略：Challenger自动生成以文档为基础的任务，Solver通过多轮检索解答。初始模型的冻结副本作为自评判，基于文档撰写针对性评价标准，并对回答评分，不依赖外部数据。

Result: 在Qwen2.5、Qwen3、OLMo-3三种7-8B指令微调模型和八个开放式基准测试上，SCOPE在开放式任务上提升最高达10.4分，并能达到或超越基于约9000条人工数据训练的GRPO_data。针对未见短文本问答任务，提升最高达13.8分，三种模型均完全超越GRPO_data。消融实验表明，Challenger协同进化使任务难度始终匹配Solver边界，检索与生成两方向能力均提升且占比随任务变化，自评标准质量仍是关键瓶颈。

Conclusion: SCOPE实现了在无数据条件下提升大模型理解与开放式生成能力，为大模型自我进化提供有效范式。

Abstract: Self-play can train language models without external supervision. However, existing methods require rule-checkable answers, leaving open-ended tasks dependent on curated prompts or frontier-model judges. We introduce SCOPE, a data-free self-play framework for open-ended tasks that co-evolves two policies: a Challenger that generates document-grounded tasks, and a Solver that answers them through multi-turn retrieval. A frozen copy of the initial model serves as the self-judge, which writes task-specific rubrics from the source document and grades Solver responses against them. Across three 7-8B instruction-tuned models (Qwen2.5, Qwen3, OLMo-3), SCOPE improves open-ended performance by up to +10.4 points on eight benchmarks and matches or exceeds GRPO_data trained on ~9K curated prompts. Although trained only on open-ended tasks, SCOPE also improves held-out short-form QA by up to +13.8 points on seven held-out benchmarks, surpassing GRPO_data on all three models. Ablations show that co-evolving the Challenger is necessary to keep tasks near the Solver's frontier, that gains arise from improvements in both retrieval and synthesis with the relative contribution varying by task, and that rubric generation quality is the bottleneck for self-judging.

### [209] [Fine-grained Verification via Diagnostic Reasoning Supervision for Aspect Sentiment Triplet Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31446)
*Wenna Lai,Haoran Xie,Guandong Xu,Qing Li,S. Joe Qin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往的三元组抽取方法侧重端到端抽取，缺乏对生成结果的细致验证，导致系统整体可靠性受限，尤其在三元组候选结果存在多层次不合理和可用性有梯度的情况下，急需一种可区分、可筛选的验证机制。

Method: 构建FiVeD框架，训练多目标校验器，主任务包括有效性分类和质量评分，辅以错误类型分类和推理理由生成。定义错误的层次类别，设计语义/语法受限下的错误三元组，并利用大型语言模型按特定标准生产评分与推理，最终依靠评分对候选结果进行筛选和重排序。

Conclusion: 细粒度验证框架FiVeD能够多角度强化ASTE系统的结果可靠性，支持可调精确率-召回权衡，可广泛用于现有三元组抽取方法中。

Abstract: Aspect Sentiment Triplet Extraction (ASTE) aims to identify aspect terms, opinion terms, and sentiment polarities as structured triplets, providing essential inputs for downstream information system applications such as opinion mining, explainable recommendations, and review summarization. Prior work mainly focuses on end-to-end extraction, while post hoc verification of extracted triplets remains comparatively underexplored. This gap limits the reliability of ASTE systems, since predicted triplets may be locally plausible while being globally invalid. Moreover, candidate invalidity is multi-faceted and candidate usability is inherently graded, motivating a fine-grained verification mechanism that can filter or re-rank outputs from diverse extractors. In this paper, we propose FiVeD, a framework for Fine-grained Verification with Diagnostic reasoning supervision. Specifically, the verifier is trained with multiple complementary objectives, including validity classification and quality score estimation as primary tasks, with error type classification and rationale generation as auxiliary tasks. We define hierarchical error categories and construct plausible incorrect triplets under semantic and syntactic constraints, and leverage an off-the-shelf LLM with task-specific rubrics to produce quality scores and diagnostic rationales. During inference, the resulting quality scores are used to filter candidate outputs, supporting adjustable precision-recall tradeoffs. Experiments across multiple ASTE baselines demonstrate that FiVeD consistently improves extraction performance by up to 3.53 F1 points as a plug-and-play verification module.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对LLM是否能够像人类一样理解并组合解释复杂自然语言表达有疑问。本文希望通过更细致的任务区分和实验来深化对模型组合能力的理解。

Method: 采用Personal Relation Task，要求测试主体解释名词短语（如“Amber's parent's friend”），分别回答结构化表达式（内涵任务）和具体对象（外延任务）。对比了人类与LLM的表现。

Result: 人类在外延任务（具体对象指代）表现更好，而LLM在内涵任务（结构化表达式）表现更好，形成鲜明对比。

Abstract: Do neural models, such as Large Language Models, genuinely acquire compositional abilities for interpretation of natural language? When we talk about semantic interpretation, we can distinguish two complementary aspects: establishing what an expression refers to in the world (which we call the Extensional task) and representing its sense in a structured way (which we call the Intensional task). We evaluate LLMs and humans on both tasks in the setting of the Personal Relation Task (Paperno 2022) in which, given a universe of people and their relationships with each other, one is asked to interpret a noun phrase such as "Amber's parent's friend". Here, for the Intensional task, the answer is the formula "friend(parent(amber))", and for the Extensional task, the person. We find that humans and LLMs show opposite strengths: humans perform better on Extensional than Intensional tasks, and LLMs vice versa. Our methodology brings greater nuance to the understanding of compositional abilities in modern machine learning models. Our results support the notion that the lack of referential grounding in LLM training is a crucial missing component in mimicking human-like language understanding.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管孟加拉语是世界第六大语言，但此前缺乏系统性评估大模型幻觉现象的工作。

Method: 构建了一个覆盖生成式问答、孟加拉-英语混合问答、摘要和推理四类任务的细粒度评测框架。使用GPT-5.4自动生成1.2万个幻觉案例，并基于三大孟加拉语数据集，引入双轨道（真值/幻觉检测）评测协议，并提出综合指标BenHalluScore。

Result: 七种模型的BenHalluScore分数在7.72%到55.42%之间，表现出幻觉检测能力巨大差异。链式思维提示（CoT）虽然改变了输出分布，但未能显著提升幻觉区分能力。

Abstract: Despite Bengali being the sixth most spoken language in the world, no prior work has systematically evaluated hallucination in large language models (LLMs) for Bengali. We construct 12,000 hallucinated candidates using GPT-5.4 across twelve task-specific hallucination types, drawn from three existing Bengali datasets, and evaluate seven LLMs spanning reasoning-oriented, multilingual, and Bengali-centric categories under a dual-track protocol that independently measures false-positive rate on ground-truth instances (Track A) and hallucination detection rate on hallucinated candidates (Track B). To jointly penalise both failure modes and prevent inflated scores from uniform response bias, we propose BenHalluScore, a dual-track calibration metric that ranges from 7.72% to 55.42% across models and tasks, revealing substantial variation in hallucination calibration. Chain-of-thought prompting, applied as a mitigation strategy, shifts response distributions without consistently improving hallucination discrimination. BenHalluEval establishes the first dedicated hallucination benchmark for Bengali and highlights the inadequacy of single-track and prompting-only evaluation approaches for low-resource language settings. The dataset and code are available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/BanglaHalluEval-EB77.

### [214] [Are Full Rollouts Necessary for On-Policy Distillation?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31490)
*Yaocheng Zhang,Jiajun Chai,Songjun Tu,Yuqian Fu,Xiaohan Wang,Wei Lin,Guojun Yin,Qichao Zhang,Yuanheng Zhu,Dongbin Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出通过控制on-policy distillation（OPD）中的rollout horizon，可以有效提升长时推理任务的训练效率，并提出两种简单有效的horizon控制策略（POPD和TOPD），显著减少算力和内存消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准OPD虽然能提供密集的教师反馈，但生成完整rollout计算代价高，且后期反馈可能不可靠。作者认为OPD的关键瓶颈在于rollout horizon，希望通过减少不必要的rollout来提高训练效率。

Method: 提出两种rollout horizon控制策略：(1) Progressive OPD（POPD）：训练过程中逐步增加rollout horizon；(2) Truncated OPD（TOPD）：始终在较短、可靠的rollout上进行蒸馏。通过实验评估了这两种策略在数学推理任务上的表现。

Result: POPD可提升训练效率最高达3倍；TOPD仅用10%的rollout horizon即能达到与标准OPD相当的性能，显著降低了训练时间和内存消耗。

Conclusion: 适当控制rollout horizon能显著提升OPD训练效率，是实现高效OPD的简单实用方法。

Abstract: On-policy distillation (OPD) provides dense teacher feedback along rollouts generated by the student and has emerged as a promising post-training paradigm for long-horizon reasoning. However, standard OPD typically generates full rollouts during training, which is computationally expensive and may expose the student to unreliable teacher feedback at late rollout positions, especially during early training. We identify the rollout horizon as a key bottleneck in OPD that substantially impacts training efficiency. Unlike Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), OPD does not require a complete trajectory or a final answer reward to provide learning signals. This observation suggests that full rollouts may not always be necessary for effective OPD. Motivated by this insight, we propose two simple horizon-control strategies: Progressive OPD (POPD), which gradually expands the rollout horizon during training, and Truncated OPD (TOPD), which permanently performs distillation on reliable truncated rollouts. Experiments on mathematical reasoning show that POPD improves the training efficiency of OPD by up to 3$\times$, while TOPD matches OPD performance using only 10\% of the rollout horizon, leading to substantial wall-clock and memory reductions. These results demonstrate that controlling the rollout horizon offers a simple and practical path to more efficient OPD.

### [215] [Consolidating Rewarded Perturbations for LLM Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31494)
*Zheyu Zhang,Shuo Yang,Gjergji Kasneci*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种名为CoRP（Consolidating Rewarded Perturbations）的梯度无关后训练方法，能用一次前向推理替代原有的多模型集成，在多个语言模型和任务上表现突出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有类似RandOpt的方法需要在推理时用多个经过奖励选优的模型做集成，推理开销大且不适用于自由生成任务。作者希望将这些奖励信息凝聚到一个可部署的单一模型中，简化推理流程。

Method: 作者首先分析了多任务模型奖励扰动后权重的低秩结构，然后提出了CoRP方法：它对奖励权重进行加权聚合、考虑兼容性重加权，并用保留的验证集检验，同时完全不需要对语言模型做梯度更新。

Result: 在五个规模（0.5B~8B）不同的语言模型和五类任务（包括数学、代码、创意写作）上，CoRP平均提升基线模型8.1分；用RandOpt 1/10的扰动预算，CoRP超过了单次推理的RandOpt 6.5分，且以单次推理恢复超过半数50模型集成收益。

Conclusion: CoRP大幅度降低推理复杂度，带来接近集成的性能提升，为梯度之外的模型后训练和部署提供了新途径。

Abstract: Post-training of language models is commonly framed as a sample-score-update loop implemented by gradient descent. A recent line of work, exemplified by RandOpt, relocates this loop to weight space, sampling Gaussian perturbations around a pretrained model and ensembling the top-K rewarded specialists at inference. While competitive with PPO and GRPO under matched training compute, this prediction-level ensemble incurs K forward passes per test example and does not extend cleanly to free-form generation. We ask whether the rewarded population can instead be folded into a single deployable model, replacing the inference-time ensemble with one consolidated update. A split-half analysis over 25 model-task pairs reveals reproducible low-rank structure in every case. We turn this geometry into CoRP (Consolidating Rewarded Perturbations), a gradient-free operator that combines reward-weighted aggregation, compatibility-aware reweighting, and a held-out validation gate, with no gradient flowing through the language model. Across five language models from 0.5B to 8B and five tasks covering math, code, and creative writing, CoRP improves the base model by 8.1 points on average. Using one tenth of RandOpt's perturbation budget, CoRP exceeds single-inference RandOpt by 6.5 points and recovers more than half of the gain of the 50-pass majority-vote ensemble, at one forward pass per test example.

</details>


### [216] [Reliable Multilingual Orthopedic Decision Support from Clinical Narratives: Language-Aware Adaptation and Verification-Guided Deferral](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31512)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低资源医疗环境中的骨科临床笔记往往包含专有术语、混合脚本、不完整证据和标签失衡，现有多语言决策支持系统难以应对这些挑战，因此需要一种面向实际需求、具备高可靠性的多语言文本分类方案。

Method: 作者比较了多语言transformer编码器、微调的DistilBERT基线、零样本大模型和新增适配头的IndicBERT-HPA。IndicBERT-HPA通过在原模型基础上加入语言感知的骨科适配头，增强了对临床相关信息的多语言表达能力。评估指标覆盖整体和类别别性能、AUC、AUPRC、校准、跨语种稳定性等。为提升实用性，还设计了包括置信度门控、证据一致性检查和语言风险筛查的选择性验证层。

Result: IndicBERT-HPA在自然临床数据分布下表现最优，平均Macro-F1为0.8792，Macro-AUROC为0.894，AUPRC为0.902。选择性验证层在5000条验证集上，覆盖率为72.3%时选择准确率为84.4%，Macro-F1为0.76，明显优于完全接受预测（准确率71.5%，Macro-F1为0.65）。零样本大模型在本任务下表现不及针对任务适配的编码器，且存在跨语种不稳定。

Conclusion: 本研究的可靠性导向多语言框架显著提升了骨科自由文本分类的准确率和稳定性，特别是适用于真实世界的低资源临床环境，为多语言临床辅助决策系统奠定了坚实基础，且通过显式的延期机制增强了决策可控性。

Abstract: Multilingual orthopedic decision support remains challenging in low-resource healthcare settings, where clinical narratives contain specialized terminology, mixed scripts, incomplete evidence, label imbalance and language-dependent documentation patterns. This article presents a reliability-oriented framework for classifying free-text orthopedic notes in English, Hindi and Punjabi. We compare task-aligned multilingual transformer encoders, a task-fine-tuned DistilBERT baseline, zero-shot instruction-tuned large language models (LLMs) and a domain-adaptive encoder, IndicBERT-HPA. IndicBERT-HPA augments IndicBERT with language-aware orthopedic adapter heads to support clinically relevant multilingual representation learning. Evaluation extends beyond aggregate accuracy to per-class performance, ROC-AUC, AUPRC, expected calibration error, cross-language stability and robustness under controlled balanced and natural-prevalence distributions. The evaluated zero-shot LLMs remain substantially less effective than task-adapted encoders for closed-set classification, with language-dependent instability. Under natural clinical prevalence, IndicBERT-HPA achieves the strongest overall performance, reaching an averaged Macro-F1 of 0.8792, Macro-AUROC of 0.894 and AUPRC of 0.902. We further implement a deterministic selective-verification layer combining confidence gating, evidence-consistency checking and language-risk screening. On a randomly selected held-out 5,000-record subset, it achieves 84.4% selective accuracy and 0.76 selective Macro-F1 at 72.3% coverage, compared with 71.5% accuracy and 0.65 Macro-F1 for accept-all prediction. These results support reliability-oriented multilingual clinical decision support with explicit deferral.

</details>


### [217] [If LLMs Have Human-Like Attributes, Then So Does Age of Empires II](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31514)
*Adrian de Wynter*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文质疑了将大型语言模型（LLM）赋予类似人类的心理属性（如道德、理解）的普遍做法，认为这些属性可能在其他系统或媒介中同样出现，因此并非LLM独有。作者通过在《帝国时代II》这款游戏中训练简单神经网络，说明只要底层平台足够强大，类似“人性化”的表现随处可见。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对LLM的讨论与研究普遍假定或推测其具有人类属性，如理解自然语言或道德判断，作者认为这种假定未经严格实证，且很可能产生误解。

Method: 作者在《帝国时代II》中构建并训练了一个简单的神经网络，展示即使不是LLM，其他复杂系统也可能表现出类似‘人性’的特征。同时论证需要明确、可度量的标准来讨论这些属性，否则只会流于误导。

Result: 实验与逻辑推导表明，所谓LLM的人类属性并非独有，许多复杂系统也可表现出类似属性，认为LLM独有这些属性是缺乏依据的。

Conclusion: 讨论LLM的‘人性’属性，必须基于明确观测标准且考虑底层平台。作者提出设定‘非独有性’前提（即假定这些属性并非LLM独有）来进行研究更为合理。

Abstract: Much research has been carried out on large language models (LLMs) and LLM-powered agentic workflows. However, many works within the field state emergence of, ascribe to, or assume, generalised anthropomorphic attributes to them (e.g., morality or understanding of natural language). Our goal is not to argue in favour or against the existence of these attributes, but to point out that these conclusions could be incorrect. For this we build and train a simple neural network on the videogame Age of Empires II, and note that any entity in a sufficiently-powerful substrate, such as LEGO or the Greater Boston Area, could also present such attributes. Hence, the purported anthropomorphic attributes of LLMs are empirically non-unique: although some properties (e.g., responses to prompts) could remain constant, others, such as the interpretation of their perceived behaviour, might change with the substrate. Thus, any empirically-grounded discussion requires explicit measurement criteria; otherwise the interpretation is left to the representation. We then show that assuming that these attributes exist or not in a system, independent of the substrate and in a generalised way, leads to either circular or uninformative conclusions, regardless of the experimenter's viewpoint on the subject. Finally we propose a 'null' assumption, where one assumes LLM non-uniqueness instead of assuming anthropomorphic attributes to set up an experiment, along with examples of it. We also discuss potential objections to our work, briefly survey the field, and prove that \textit{Age of Empires II} is functionally- and Turing-complete.

*Yuhan Song,Linhao Zhang,Aiwei Liu,Chuhan Wu,Sijun Zhang,Wei Jia,Yuan Liu,Houfeng Wang,Xiao Zhou*

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的语义语音分词器虽对语音任务表现良好，但由于过度关注语义抽象，难以感知和还原音频中的非语言信息，限制了其在更广泛音频任务中的应用。

Method: 提出UniAudio-Token，包含两项创新：（1）语义-声学原语（SAP）：将音频分解为语言内容、声乐属性和听觉场景要素，提供结构化监督。（2）语义-声学均衡（SAE）：通过内容感知门控机制，自适应地从模型浅层恢复精细声学细节。整体提升了分词器的声学感知能力。

Result: 在多个下游任务和评价指标下，UniAudio-Token均超过了所有单codebook分词基线模型，既保证了语音任务的表现也拓展了音频任务的适用性，实现了统一音频接口。

Conclusion: UniAudio-Token成功突破了传统语义分词器对音频理解的局限，可作为通用音频接口，相关代码和模型已开源，促进后续音频大模型的研究与应用。

Abstract: Semantic speech tokenizers have become a widely used interface for Audio-LLMs, owing to their compact single-codebook design and strong linguistic alignment. However, their focus on linguistic abstraction induces acoustic blindness, limiting their applicability beyond speech-centric tasks. We propose UniAudio-Token, a framework that empowers semantic tokenizers with general audio perception without compromising speech ability. Instead of altering the semantic paradigm, UniAudio-Token mitigates its information loss through two key innovations: (1) Semantic-Acoustic Primitives (SAP) provide structured supervision by decomposing audio into linguistic content, vocal attributes, and auditory-scene primitives; and (2) Semantic-Acoustic Equilibrium (SAE) introduces a content-aware gating mechanism that adaptively restores fine-grained acoustic details from shallow layers. Extensive evaluations show that UniAudio-Token learns comprehensive universal representations while preserving high-fidelity speech generation. When integrated with downstream LLMs, it outperforms all single-codebook baseline tokenizers on both understanding and generation tasks, effectively serving as a unified audio interface. We publicly release all our code, including training and inference scripts, together with the model checkpoints at https://github.com/Tencent/Universal_Audio_Tokenizer.

### [219] [Preference-Aware Rubric Learning for Personalized Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31545)
*Yilun Qiu,Xiaoyan Zhao,Yang Zhang,Yuxin Chen,Cilin Yan,Jiayin Cai,Xiaolong Jiang,Yao Hu,Yoko Yamakata,Tat-Seng Chua*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型（LLM）转向面向用户的智能体，个性化成了关键需求。现有评测方法难以捕捉长期互动中主观、用户特定的偏好，成为进一步推进个性化对齐的瓶颈。

Method: 作者提出将个性化评测建模为学习问题而非静态判断，创造了“个性化评测即学习”（Personalized Evaluation as Learning）的新范式。具体方法为PARL：直接从用户交互历史中归纳出关注偏好的评测标准（rubric），通过判别式强化学习目标，使评测标准能清晰反映用户响应与个性化模型产出之间的界限，并对偏好一致性进行自我验证。

Result: 实验证明，PARL在真实任务上能够稳定学习出高保真度的个性化评测标准，既可准确识别用户偏好，同时表现出良好的泛化性，能捕捉用户风格及细粒度评判模式。

Conclusion: PARL首次实现了从历史数据中自动归纳用户个性化评测标准，为LLM个性化对齐提供可靠评估工具，为今后相关研究及应用带来巨大推动。

Abstract: As Large Language Models (LLMs) evolve from general-purpose assistants to user-centric agents, personalization has become central to aligning model behavior with individual preferences, making the evaluation of personalized alignment a critical bottleneck. Existing evaluation methods-ranging from automatic metrics to LLM-as-a-judge approaches-fail to capture subjective, user-specific preferences embedded in long-term interaction histories. We identify three essential principles for reliable and effective personalized evaluation: Representativeness, User-Consistency, and Discriminativeness. To address these principles, we introduce Personalized Evaluation as Learning, a paradigm that formulates personalized evaluation as a learning problem rather than a static judgment. Under this paradigm, we propose PARL (Preference-Aware Rubric Learning for Personalized Evaluation), a framework that learns to induce preference-aware evaluation rubrics directly from raw user histories and performs a self-validation mechanism to ensure consistency with the user's preferences. PARL integrates rubric induction with a discriminative reinforcement learning objective that contrasts user-authored responses against competitive personalized model outputs, enabling the learned rubrics to capture precise, user-specific decision boundaries. Experiments on real-world personalized text generation tasks show that PARL consistently induces high-fidelity rubrics that reliably identify user-aligned responses and generalize across users and tasks, while capturing stable stylistic preferences and fine-grained evaluative patterns. To ensure reproducibility, our code is available at https://github.com/SnowCharmQ/PARL.

### [220] [Semantic Triplet Restoration: A Novel Protocol for Hierarchical Table Understanding in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31550)
*Yibin Zhao,Fangxin Shang,Dingrui Yang,Yuqi Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Semantic Triplet Restoration (STR)的新协议，用于提升表格问答任务中的推理效率和准确性。STR通过将表格每个单元格转写为语义三元组，更精确表达表语义并减少输入长度。实验显示方法在多个中英文基准上均表现优异，尤其适合小模型和长表格情境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有表格问答模型常用HTML/Markdown等序列化方式表达表格，但这类方式增加了标记复杂性和推理难度，特别是在表格包含合并单元格、层级表头等复杂结构时，对模型的推理能力消耗极大。因此，亟需一种能显式表达表格语义关系、降低推理负担的高效表示方法。

Method: 作者提出STR协议，将每个单元格转为<item path, feature path, value>三元组，显式表示行实体、列属性和单元格值，并设计了TripletQL路由模块，能根据提问场景筛选、渲染相关三元组子集，简化模型推理流程。

Result: 在四个中英文表格问答基准测试上，STR方法在准确率上达到或超过基于HTML的主流方法，并有效减少了输入token数目。优势在模型规模较小或表格长度较长时更为显著。

Conclusion: STR显式的三元组表示法简化了表格中的语义推理，降低大模型推理成本，对受算力约束场景特别有效，有望在表格理解与问答等任务中得到广泛应用。

Abstract: Table question answering requires models to recover semantic relations encoded implicitly by two-dimensional layout, merged cells, and hierarchical headers. Current pipelines typically use HTML or Markdown as intermediate table representations, but these layout-oriented serializations introduce markup overhead and require large language models to infer header-cell alignments from row and column spans. We propose Semantic Triplet Restoration (STR), a protocol that rewrites each cell as an atomic fact <item path, feature path, value>, where the item path specifies the row-wise entity, the feature path specifies the hierarchical attribute, and the value contains the cell content. We also present TripletQL, a lightweight query-aware router that uses STR to select an appropriate rendering or filtered subset of triplets for each question. Across four Chinese and English table-QA benchmarks, STR matches or improves upon HTML-based baselines while reducing input tokens. The relative benefit grows for smaller language models and longer table contexts, suggesting that explicit semantic representations are especially useful under constrained inference budgets. Code and data are available at https://github.com/Phoenix-ni/STR.git .

### [221] [What Am I Missing? Question-Answering as Hidden State Probing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31561)
*Chu Fei Luo,Samuel Dahan,Xiaodan Zhu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文提出通过“提问”作为推理干预手段，发现语言模型在问题生成阶段即已自我诊断出正确性信号，并探讨利用该信号提升答案准确率，但干预对正确与错误推理路径影响均等，表明模型自我修正能力有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型（LLM）在链式思维推理方面表现突出，但其推理过程中机制仍不透明，尤其是同一提示下输出结果存在随机性。作者希望借助提问机制更好地揭示并利用模型推理过程中的隐藏状态信息。

Method: 作者提出学生-教师模式：学生在解答问题时向教师提问，通过分析学生在提问前后的隐藏状态，训练探测器用于预测最终答案的正确性，并构建“提问”门控策略来指导推理过程。

Result: 实验发现，通过隐藏状态的自我诊断信号可有效预测答案正确性，但提问干预对正确和错误推理路径的恢复和损伤概率基本相当，未能显著提升整体推理准确率。

Conclusion: 模型自身在不确定性下的自我校正能力有限，单纯利用问题生成阶段的信息进行干预尚不足以大幅提升最终解答质量，对后续自我提升方法设计提出挑战。

Abstract: Test-time reasoning has become a significant field of study since the introduction of chain-of-thought reasoning in large language models (LLMs). However, the mechanisms of this reasoning process are still under-explored -- from the same input prompt, and even the same partial solution, LLMs can produce varied answers if sampled multiple times. We propose to leverage question-asking as an inference-time intervention that articulates information about the model's hidden state. To achieve that, we present a student-teacher setting where a student asks questions to a teacher. We train a probe on the student's hidden state before and after asking a question and find it is predictive of the trajectory's final correctness, even before generating the teacher's answer. This suggests there is a meaningful signal from the self-diagnosis that occurs during question generation rather than information transfer from the teacher. We then frame question-asking as a sequential decision problem, using this probe as a quality score, and define a gating policy to ask questions that maximize likelihood of correctness. We find that the success of question-asking as an intervention is largely dependent on the model's self-consistency. Our empirical results show a gap between detection and recovery; while our gating policy captures model correctness and uncertainty, interventions are equally likely to harm correct trajectories as they are to recover incorrect ones. This gap between diagnosis and correction has broader implications on language models' capacity for self-refinement under uncertainty.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者统一了不同的模型、训练策略、损失函数和评价指标，横跨标签和解释的多种表示空间（硬、软、中间），并系统重实现各种度量方法。分类指标聚焦于预测性和分布性，解释性指标分为可信度、忠实度和复杂度三维。

Abstract: Human disagreement is ubiquitous and well-known in labeling. However, variation in explanations, captured through token-level human rationales, remains far less explored. At the same time, it is unclear how to best evaluate human labels and rationales -- or even how to best aggregate rationales beyond majority vote -- in light of this variation. Yet, rationales may provide additional insights into the richness of human reasoning, that may differ in style, values and interpretations -- especially in subjective NLP tasks like hate speech detection. In this work, we unify diverse models, training strategies, loss functions, and existing evaluation metrics under a single protocol by systematically re-implementing them across different label and rationale representation spaces. Classification metrics are organized around two key properties -- predictive and distributional -- while explainability metrics through three complementary dimensions: plausibility, faithfulness, and complexity. In this unified supervision framework, we evaluate model behavior across classification and explainability metrics, as well as metric sensitivity to the choice of label (hard and soft) and rationale representation space (hard, intermediate and soft). Results show that both hard and soft metrics favor softer representations, highlighting their effectiveness in capturing variation and the need to rethink evaluation in subjective NLP.

### [223] [What Gets Unmasked First? Trajectory Analysis of Diffusion Models for Graph-to-Text Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31564)
*Qing Wang,Jacob Devasier,Chengkai Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文系统性研究了面向图到文本生成的掩码扩散语言模型（MDLM）。作者分析了MDLM的生成轨迹，并提出了一种改进推理方法以及新的模型结构，显著提升了生成质量和泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前主流自回归大模型在图到文本任务上生成方式受限，掩码扩散语言模型（MDLM）的生成机制和优势仍未充分研究。此外，现有的模型容易过拟合于特定数据集。作者旨在填补这一空白，同时提升生成泛化能力。

Method: 1）系统研究MDLM的生成轨迹并与自回归模型对比；2）发现并分析了监督微调（SFT）破坏MDLM生成策略的现象；3）提出lambda缩放结构性解码，在推理时降低结构Token置信度，无需重新训练；4）引入Graph-LLaDA，将图Transformer编码器集成到LLaDA中以显式利用图结构信息。

Result: lambda缩放结构性解码显著提升了BLEU-4分数（+9.4），Graph-LLaDA在LAGRANGE等多数据集测试中表现出比以往baseline更强的泛化能力，优于过拟合数据集的传统模型。

Abstract: We present the first systematic study of masked diffusion language models (MDLMs) for graph-to-text generation. We analyze MDLM generation trajectories -- the order in which tokens are unmasked during iterative decoding -- and find that, unlike autoregressive LLMs which generate text linearly, MDLMs naturally prioritize entities first, followed by relational and function words, with structural tokens resolved last. We further identify a previously undocumented failure mode of supervised fine-tuning: SFT disrupts this strategy by prematurely anchoring structural sentence-ending tokens early in the decoding trajectory, effectively fixing the output length which can lead to omitted or hallucinated information. To address this, we propose lambda-scaled structural decoding, a training-free inference-time modification that downweights structural token confidence and recovers +9.4 BLEU-4. Finally, we introduce Graph-LLaDA, which integrates a Graph Transformer encoder into LLaDA's decoding process to explicitly incorporate relational graph structure. Cross-dataset evaluation on LAGRANGE reveals that previous baselines overfit to dataset-specific patterns, while LLM- and MDLM-based approaches generalize significantly better.

### [224] [LongTraceRL: Learning Long-Context Reasoning from Search Agent Trajectories with Rubric Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31584)
*Nianyi Lin,Jiajie Zhang,Lei Hou,Juanzi Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新方法（LongTraceRL），通过设计更具挑战性的干扰数据和细粒度奖励，显著提升了大语言模型在长上下文推理任务中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型在需要处理大量相关与无关信息的长文本推理任务时常常失败，现有基于强化学习的方案存在干扰项可混淆性弱及奖励稀疏、难以中间过程监督等问题。

Method: 1）数据构建时，通过知识图谱随机游走生成多跳推理问题，并根据智能体的搜索轨迹构建分层干扰文档（高低可混淆性）；2）设计了一种基于金标准实体链路的rubric reward，对推理过程中的每一跳提供实体级别的奖励（只对完全正确的最终回答施加），用于细粒度监督，区分不同正确推理路径的质量。

Result: 在三个规模（4B-30B参数）的LLMs以及五个长上下文推理基准测试上，LongTraceRL在多项指标上均优于现有强大基线，显著提升模型的基于证据的全面推理能力。

Conclusion: 本文提出的LongTraceRL方法能更有效地训练LLM进行复杂的长上下文推理，推动了相关任务中模型能力的提升，并对未来基于推理和信息整合的下游任务具有应用价值。

Abstract: Long-context reasoning remains a central challenge for large language models, which often fail to locate and integrate key information in extensive distracting content. Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has shown promise for this task, yet existing methods are limited by low-confusability distractors and sparse, outcome-only reward signals that cannot supervise intermediate reasoning steps. To address these issues, we introduce \textsc{LongTraceRL}. For data construction, we generate multi-hop questions via knowledge graph random walks and leverage search agent trajectories to build \emph{tiered distractors}: documents the agent read but did not cite (high confusability) and documents that appeared in search results but were never opened (low confusability), producing training contexts that are far more challenging than those built by random sampling or one-shot search. For reward design, we propose a \emph{rubric reward} that uses the gold entities along each reasoning chain as fine-grained, entity-level process supervision. This rubric reward is applied only to responses with correct final answers (positive-only strategy), distinguishing the reasoning quality among correct responses and preventing reward hacking. Experiments on three reasoning LLMs (4B--30B) across five long-context benchmarks demonstrate that \textsc{LongTraceRL} consistently outperforms strong baselines and encourages comprehensive, evidence-grounded reasoning. Codes, datasets and models are available at \href{https://github.com/THU-KEG/LongTraceRL}{https://github.com/THU-KEG/LongTraceRL}.

</details>


### [225] [Language Models Learn Constructional Semantics, Not To Mention Syntax: Investigating LM Understanding of Paired-Focus Constructions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31586)
*Wesley Scivetti,Ethan Wilcox,Nathan Schneider,Kanishka Misra,Leonie Weissweiler*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文探讨了开源语言模型对英语中罕见的Paired-Focus句式（如“let alone”、“much less”）的语义理解能力，并证明中等规模的开源模型在特定条件下可掌握这类构式的形式与意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解罕见语言构式的语义对自然语言处理非常重要。目前只有最大型的LLM才能较好地处理这类问题，尚不明确开源模型是否能有效理解这种构式及其学习机制。

Method: 作者构建了一个新数据集，测试了多种模型（涵盖参数量、架构、数据集规模等差异）对罕见Paired-Focus句式的理解，包括形态和语义测试，结合形容词刻度语义和常识世界知识；并分析了部分开源模型训练过程中的学习动态。

Result: 一些中等规模的模型能敏感感知Paired-Focus构式的形式和意义，而仅在“人类规模”数据下训练的模型在语义测试中表现失败。训练动态分析显示，Paired-Focus语义理解出现较晚，且与世界知识学习提升相关。

Conclusion: 中等规模开源语言模型能够掌握罕见的Paired-Focus句式，且对这种句式的理解与其他意义领域的知识有关联。

Abstract: Grasping the semantics of rare constructions (form-meaning pairings) has been shown to be a challenging problem that has currently only been solved by the largest LLMs. It remains an open question if open-source models have robust constructional understanding, and if so, what learning dynamics underlie the acquisition of this knowledge. Focusing on a set of rare Paired-Focus constructions in English (e.g. "let alone", "much less"), we construct a novel dataset to test their meanings using both scalar adjectival semantics and general world knowledge. Testing a wide range of models differing in parameter count, architecture, and pretraining dataset size, we find that several modestly sized models are sensitive to both the forms and the meanings of Paired-Focus constructions, though models trained on human-scale data fail at all meaning evaluations. Turning to training dynamics for a set of open-checkpoint models, we find that Paired-Focus understanding emerges later in training than Paired-Focus syntactic knowledge, and that learning of Paired-Focus semantics is correlated with gains in some domains of world knowledge. Overall, our empirical results support the conclusion that modestly sized open-source models can grasp the rare Paired-Focus constructions, and demonstrate a connection between knowledge of Paired-Focus constructions and other meaning domains.

</details>

### [226] [Structured interactions improve distributed coordination beyond model scaling in a real-world multi-robot system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30383)
*Junping Wang,Zhizhong Zhang,Yongqiang Tang,Geng Zheng,Jiaming Zhang,Shiji Song,Yanmei Li,Yushan Ma*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 与单纯提升单个机器人能力相比，优化多机器人系统中的通信结构，在硬件预算相同的情况下带来更显著的性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统提升机器人系统性能的方法往往聚焦于提升单个机器人的感知、决策模型规模，但这增加了成本。本研究关注于在预算一致的前提下，通过调整机器人间的通信拓扑，是否能够获得比扩大单体模型更大的系统性能提升。

Method: 在一个包含10台实体机器人的搬运与建图任务上进行实验，通过变更通信拓扑结构（完全连接 vs. 模块化分层），并比较扩大神经网络隐层规模的效果，采用混合效应模型分析各条件下的性能提升。部分实验在SMAC平台独立复现，并对异构任务数据进行一致性验证。

Result: 将通信结构从完全连接切换为模块化分层，系统性能提升47分；扩大神经网络规模，最多仅提升9分。模型拟合优度显示，通信结构对性能的影响显著大于神经网络规模。模拟外推中，模型规模达到1024隐层单元后效果趋于饱和。

Conclusion: 在多机器人系统和任务设定下，合理设计交互结构比单纯扩展单体模型规模对系统性能提升作用更大。但结论的广泛适用性还需要进一步量化和验证。

Abstract: Scaling individual robot capabilities is common but costly. Here we investigate a system-level design question in real-world multi-robot coordination: given matched hardware budgets, does restructuring communication among robots yield larger gains than increasing onboard model size? Using a representative transport-and-mapping task with 10 physical robots (5 runs per condition, 60 runs total), we find that switching from fully connected to modular hierarchical interactions improves normalised performance by 47 points (0--100), whereas doubling neural network hidden size yields at most 9 points. Nested mixed-effects model comparisons show a substantially larger improvement in model fit for topology than for scale. The pattern is confirmed in independent SMAC replications; heterogeneous benchmark reanalyses provide secondary supporting consistency checks rather than primary evidence. Performance saturation beyond 1024 hidden units is observed in simulation-calibrated extrapolation, not directly on hardware. These results indicate that interaction structure can play a dominant role within the tested system and task setting, while broader quantitative generalisation remains to be established.

</details>


### [227] [Learning-Based Navigation for Indoor Mobile Robots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30468)
*Tri-Tin Nguyen,Tien-Dat Nguyen,Gia-Uy Le,Vinh Nguyen,Vinh-Hao Nguyen*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于学习的室内移动机器人导航框架，将神经网络的全局路径规划与强化学习优化的局部路径规划相结合，有效提升了导航的安全性和可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前室内移动机器人在复杂环境中的自主导航面临全局路径规划与局部运动控制之间的有效结合难题，传统方法常受限于手工启发式和局部最优，难以兼顾全局性与安全性。为此，作者旨在利用深度学习与强化学习技术提升导航智能化水平。

Method: 方法上，作者采用两级架构：全局部分，利用专家A*轨迹生成并训练带有代价感知的神经网络全局规划器；局部部分，提出基于离散动态窗口（DWA）动作网格的选择，通过行为克隆进行初步训练，随后引入PPO算法结合可行性掩码进行策略优化。该框架在仿真与实际室内环境中均实现并测试。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法能够输出可行的全局路径，并在障碍物存在下产生可靠且安全的局部动作指令，助力目标导向的准确导航，优于传统方法。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了基于学习的全局-局部导航集成策略的可行性和优越性，为室内移动机器人安全自主导航提供了新思路，代码已开源以促进进一步研究。

Abstract: This paper presents a learning-based navigation framework for indoor mobile robots. The proposed method combines a supervised neural global planner, trained from cost-aware A* expert trajectories, with the proposed Learning-Based DWA local planner, which is formulated as discrete candidate selection over the Dynamic Window Approach (DWA) action lattice. For local planning, the policy is first trained by behavior cloning and then refined by Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) under feasibility-aware masking. The framework is implemented and evaluated in both simulated and real-world indoor environments. Experimental results show that the proposed method generates feasible global routes and reliable local motion commands for safe goal-directed navigation in the presence of obstacles. These results demonstrate the effectiveness of integrating learning-based global planning with reinforcement-learning-refined local control for indoor mobile robot navigation. The source code will be released at https://ntdathp.github.io/rl_robot_web/.

</details>


### [228] [ELAN4D: Embodiment-Centric 4D Supervision for Vision-Language-Action Models via Plug-and-Play Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30484)
*Zeyuan He,Bowen Yang,Zhirui Fang,Keru Zhou,Lei Jiang,Jingjing Qian,Fan Mo,Junchi Yan,Philip Torr,Xiu Li,Li Jiang,Jialin Yu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: ELAN4D是一种用于机器人操控的训练框架，通过引入未来机器人关键点的运动轨迹（4D监督），显著提升了视觉-语言-动作模型在各种分布扰动下的泛化和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA（视觉-语言-动作）模型多为直接从观测回归动作的反应式策略，缺乏对未来动力学的显式建模，导致在异常扰动（如摄像头、背景、布局变化）下泛化能力有限。

Method: 提出ELAN4D框架：利用机器人的前向运动学，仅用本体状态推导出关键点（如关节、末端执行器）的3D运动轨迹，将其作为紧凑、度量化的4D时空监督，通过轻量解码器以辅助分支插入到动作专家模块，同时对预训练的视觉-语言骨干进行梯度隔离以保持其能力，推理阶段无需该辅助分支。

Result: 在LIBERO、LIBERO-Plus、RoboTwin2.0和实际操控任务中，ELAN4D在多种强基线模型之上均带来持续和显著提升，特别是在面对应激扰动（摄像头、背景、布局等变化）时表现出更高的鲁棒性和泛化能力。

Conclusion: 基于本体感知的4D时空监督能有效增强VLA模型在复杂环境中的泛化和鲁棒性，为构建更加健壮和通用的机器人操控策略提供了新思路。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have shown promise for robotic manipulation, yet most existing policies operate reactively by directly regressing actions from current observations, without explicitly modeling future dynamics. This limits their ability to generalize under out-of-distribution perturbations. To address this issue, we propose ELAN4D, an embodiment-centric, 4D-aware training framework that enhances VLA policies with future robot keypoint tracks as predictive spatio-temporal supervision. Using only forward kinematics from proprioceptive states, we derive 3D displacement tracks of robot keypoints, such as joints and the end-effector, with negligible preprocess cost. These tracks provide metric and compact supervision without requiring external trackers or reconstruction. A plug-and-play auxiliary branch with a lightweight track decoder injects this 4D signal into the action expert while preserving the pretrained vision-language backbone through gradient isolation. The track decoder is discarded during inference, leaving the base policy interface unchanged. Extensive experiments on LIBERO, LIBERO-Plus, RoboTwin2.0 and real-world manipulation tasks demonstrate that ELAN4D consistently improves over strong VLA baselines, achieving the best overall performance and substantial gains under out-of-distribution perturbations, including camera, background, and layout shifts. These results highlight the effectiveness of embodiment-centric 4D supervision for building more robust and generalizable manipulation policies.

</details>


### [229] [CoMo3R-SLAM: Collaborative Monocular Dense SLAM with Learned 3D Reconstruction Priors for Outdoor Multi-Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30488)
*Zhihao Cao,Qi Shao,Shuhao Zhai,Feng Tian,Anh Nguyen,Hesheng Wang,Baoru Huang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该论文提出了CoMo3R-SLAM，这是首个支持多人协作的基于单目RGB相机的稠密SLAM系统，无需深度传感器即可实现大规模户外环境下多机器人协同建图。系统在多个公开数据集上表现优异，有效提升了单目协作SLAM的精度和实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多机器人协作SLAM系统多依赖深度传感器，成本高、配置复杂，而单目相机虽然轻便，但存在尺度不确定性、跨主体特征关联难等问题，传统方法在户外场景低重叠、重复结构条件下表现不佳，因此亟需能在户外环境中实现鲁棒、准确协作单目SLAM的新技术。

Method: 提出CoMo3R-SLAM系统，每个机器人前端基于预训练先验进行实时追踪和局部稠密融合；中心协调器负责密集点云匹配、Sim(3)同步和GPU加速全局bundle adjustment，并做分段级深度优化，无需深度传感器或已知内参，全流程基于RGB单目输入。

Result: 在Tanks and Temples和Waymo公开数据集上测试，CoMo3R-SLAM在3/4个Tanks and Temples场景获得最佳ATE（绝对轨迹误差），Waymo数据也达到先进水平，甚至可媲美或超越部分RGB-D方法；系统支持8FPS在线运行。

Conclusion: CoMo3R-SLAM实现了可靠、高效的多机器人协作单目稠密SLAM，为无需深度传感器的户外多主体3D建图提供了新思路，展示了极具实际应用前景的性能和适用性。

Abstract: Collaborative dense SLAM is essential for multi-robot teams to achieve scalable and consistent 3D perception across large-scale outdoor environments. Existing systems typically depend on depth sensors, incurring significant payload, power, and calibration costs. Monocular RGB cameras are a lightweight alternative, but collaborative monocular dense SLAM remains difficult due to scale ambiguity, unreliable inter-agent data association, especially in outdoor scenes where low overlap and repetitive structures make traditional feature matching unreliable, motivating robust geometric information. We propose CoMo3R-SLAM, the first collaborative monocular dense RGB SLAM system that leverages robust learned feed-forward 3D reconstruction priors for outdoor multi-agent mapping. Each agent runs a prior-guided front-end for real-time tracking and local dense fusion, while a coordinator performs dense pointmap matching for cross-agent verification, closed-form Sim(3) gauge synchronization, and GPU-accelerated global bundle adjustment with segment-level depth optimization. Requiring neither depth sensors nor parametric intrinsics, our system produces robust cross-agent constraints and globally consistent metric maps from monocular RGB alone. On Tanks and Temples and Waymo sequences, CoMo3R-SLAM achieves the best ATE on three of four Tanks and Temples scenes and competitive Waymo accuracy, matching or exceeding state-of-the-art RGB-D methods while running online at 8 FPS.

</details>


### [230] [Physics-informed Goal-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning under Hybrid Contact Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30503)
*Vittorio Giammarino,Anastasios Manganaris,Ahmed H. Qureshi*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文分析了基于物理知识的目标条件强化学习在复杂接触操作任务中遇到的挑战，并提出了更具接触感知和层级性的改进方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目标条件强化学习（GCRL）在处理带有高维、混合或接触依赖动力学的任务时，泛化能力大幅下降，当前基于物理知识的GCRL方法在充满接触的操作任务中的表现和可靠性尚不明确。

Method: 通过理论分析指出原有物理知识嵌入的GCRL方法在复杂接触任务中容易失效，提出了接触感知和层级性的新范式，将物理启发式归纳偏置有选择地应用于操作问题的不同部分。

Result: 实验结果和理论分析显示，新的方法确实提升了Pi-GCRL在接触丰富操作任务中的表现和泛化能力。

Conclusion: 本研究推动了物理知识嵌入型目标条件强化学习在复杂接触操作领域的研究和应用边界，证明了结构化的归纳偏置和分层建模的必要性和有效性。

Abstract: Learning to reach arbitrary goals from sparse feedback requires agents to infer a rich notion of reachability across state--goal pairs. Goal-conditioned reinforcement learning (GCRL) tackles this challenge by learning policies that generalize across goals, but this generalization becomes increasingly difficult as the underlying dynamics become high-dimensional, hybrid, or contact-dependent. To address this issue, physics-informed GCRL (Pi-GCRL) introduces optimal-control-inspired inductive biases into goal-conditioned value learning. While Pi-GCRL methods have proven effective in navigation and object-free goal-reaching domains, their reliability in contact-rich tasks remains unclear, where contact interactions induce hybrid dynamics, mode-dependent controllability, and nonsmooth value landscapes. In this work, we show that these structural properties can cause existing Pi-GCRL methods to degrade when applied naively to contact-rich manipulation. Motivated by this analysis, we introduce contact-aware and hierarchical formulations that apply physics-informed inductive biases selectively across the manipulation problem. Our results provide a principled step toward extending Pi-GCRL to contact-rich manipulation.

### [231] [VLM-GLoc: Vision-Language Model Enhanced Monte Carlo Localization for Robust Semantic Global Localization in Cluttered Quasi-Static Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30506)
*Shivendra Agrawal,Bradley Hayes*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用视觉-语言模型（VLM）进行全局定位的新方法VLM-GLoc，在超市和实验室等具有几何和语义歧义的静态环境下效果突出，显著优于传统方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在超市、办公室等环境中，重复的几何结构和商品分布导致机器人定位困难。传统方法依赖特定几何特征或人工定制视觉处理，但面对长尾语义分布或视觉杂乱时表现不佳，亟需统一高效的定位方法。

Method: 提出了一种基于开放词汇视觉-语言模型（VLM）的分层语义蒙特卡洛定位（MCL）方法。其创新之处包括：用VLM抽取丰富区分性的文本特征，自动过滤模糊和动态目标，并通过文本-地图检索反向种子生成粒子，实现更高效的语义级粒子采样。

Result: 在两种实际环境、两个平台（手机和四足机器人）上的实验中，VLM-GLoc全局定位成功率分别达到70%和74%，显著优于几何特征和特定领域基线方法。

Conclusion: VLM-GLoc验证了开放词汇视觉-语言模型在复杂室内环境中的应用潜力，能有效提升移动机器人在充满歧义场景下的全局定位能力，为机器人室内自主导航带来新思路。

Abstract: Global localization in geometrically aliased, quasi-static environments such as grocery stores, offices, schools, and hospitals poses a significant challenge for mobile robots. Grocery stores with parallel aisles and a long tailed distribution of products, as well as offices and labs with repetitive furniture such as chairs, desks, monitors, and doors, exemplify common indoor environments that present geometric and even semantic ambiguity. Traditional approaches rely either on distinct geometric features or on domain-specific vision pipelines that struggle with long-tail semantic distributions and transient visual clutter. We present VLM-GLoc, a method for hierarchical semantic Monte Carlo Localization (MCL) that leverages open-vocabulary Vision-Language Models (VLMs) as a unified semantic observation front-end. We hypothesize a three-fold benefit from VLMs: (1) extracting highly discriminative rich text features, (2) implicit quality filtering of blurry or dynamic objects, and (3) permanence reasoning for targeted data augmentation. We introduce an inverse semantic proposal mechanism that seeds particles via text-to-map retrieval. Evaluated across two real-world environments with different characteristics and two different platforms: a 3,500 sq. ft. grocery store with a cellphone and a 3,700 sq. ft. lab space with a quadruped, VLM-GLoc achieves 70% and 74% global localization success respectively, substantially outperforming traditional geometry-only and domain-specific baselines.

</details>


### [232] [ARISTO Hand: Sensing-Driven Distal Hyperextension for Fine-Grained Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30508)
*Aaron Kim,Dong Ho Kang,Mark Helwig,Mingyo Seo,Kazuto Yokoyama,Tetsuya Narita,Luis Sentis*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新型腱驱仿人机械手ARISTO Hand，结合主动远端过伸能力和混合指尖传感架构，用于精细薄物体操作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精细操作薄物体需要精准的接触几何和可靠的力感知，但现有仿人机械手在机械结构和传感能力上存在不足，难以胜任这类任务。

Method: ARISTO Hand采用主动远端过伸设计，能让指尖动作超出标准屈伸极限。同时，手指集成了刚性指甲力矩传感器和柔性电容触觉阵列，实现混合式力觉与触觉感知。对机械手的受力特性进行了量化评测，并在SD卡多阶段插拔任务中进行了实验验证。

Result: 主动过伸显著提升了夹薄物能力（对1-20mm物体厚度，拉出力提升2.76倍）。刚性传感器在接触边缘时可获得稳定力估计，在发生运动学奇异点时性能优于本体力觉。

Conclusion: 所提出的机械手架构兼具高灵活性与可靠力感知，可大幅提升机器人操作薄物体的精准性和可靠性，为未来机器人精细操作提供了新思路。

Abstract: Manipulating thin objects requires precise contact geometry and reliable force perception, yet many anthropomorphic robotic hands lack the mechanical and sensing capabilities needed for such interactions. We present the ARISTO Hand, a tendon-driven robotic hand that integrates active distal hyperextension with a hybrid fingertip-sensing architecture that combines a rigid, nail-mounted force-torque sensor and a soft capacitive tactile array. Active hyperextension enables controlled fingertip engagement beyond the kinematic limits of standard flexion, increasing pull-out force by 2.76x for object thicknesses of 1-20 mm while preserving the nominal grasp capability. The rigid nail-mounted sensor provides reliable force measurements during edge contacts, where the sensitivity of proprioceptive force estimation degrades as the contact geometry approaches kinematic singularities. We validate the proposed architecture through quantitative force characterization and a multi-stage SD card extraction and insertion task. Video and supplementary materials are available at: https://aristohand.github.io

</details>


### [233] [Any-ttach: Quick End-effector Swapping Enables Manipulation Dexterity with Simplicity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30569)

Method: Any-ttach框架由三部分组成：1）一种低成本、自动化的末端执行器快速切换机制（开关式）；2）用于采集人类示范的手持设备；3）兼容已学习参数化和规划的工具使用技能的任务规划框架。该系统支持多种工具和模块（如日常工具、剪刀等关节工具、仿生手等）并利用统一接口切换。

Any-ttach combines a low-cost automatic swapping mechanism for an open-close robot interface, a handheld device for collecting human demonstrations, and a task planning framework that composes learned, parameterized, and planned tool-use skills. The system supports diverse tools and end-effector modules, including daily tools, articulated tools such as scissors, Fin Ray fingers, and a low-cost anthropomorphic hand, through the same shared interface. Our experiments show that Any-ttach improves tool-swapping reliability, increases demonstration efficiency, reduces tool-pose variability, and supports diverse tool-use skills. More details and videos are available at https://any-ttach.github.io/.

### [234] [Caspar: CUDA Accelerator for Symbolic Programming with Adaptive Reordering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30583)
*Emil Martens,Aaron Miller,Matias Varnum,Annette Stahl*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: Caspar是一个将Python符号化编程与高性能CUDA GPU计算桥接的库，实现了先进的非线性优化GPU求解器，显著提升了比如大规模Bundle Adjustment等问题的效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代机器人及优化问题对计算效率的需求日益增加，而GPU加速能力难以直接为符号化编程和复杂优化建模服务，本工作致力于简化开发流程并提升性能。

Method: 基于SymForce库，用户用Python编写符号表达式，Caspar自动将其转译为高效的CUDA内核代码并在GPU运行，支持Lie群等运算，同时只需定义符号残差函数，无需手写梯度推导。

Result: 在大规模Bundle Adjustment基准（BAL）测试中，与同类最先进方法相比，Caspar在速度上快5至20倍、内存占用更少，准确度相当。

Conclusion: Caspar显著降低了高性能非线性优化任务开发难度，优化效率极高，适用于各种机器人领域的大规模优化问题，相关代码已经开源。

Abstract: We present Caspar, a library that makes the power of modern GPUs more accessible in robotics and provides a state-of-the-art nonlinear GPU solver that can be applied to a wide range of different optimization problems. Caspar bridges the gap between expressive symbolic programming in Python and high-performance GPU runtimes in C++ by automatically generating optimized CUDA kernels from symbolic expressions. Building on the SymForce library, users can easily define and combine symbolic expressions, including Lie group operations, to generate custom CUDA kernels. To use Caspar as a solver, users need only define the symbolic residual functions; Caspar then uses symbolic differentiation to generate the necessary GPU kernels and interfaces to perform nonlinear optimization.
  In this paper, we present the core components of Caspar and showcase its performance by performing bundle adjustment on the Bundle Adjustment in the Large (BAL) dataset. We benchmark Caspar against other state-of-the-art bundle adjusters and show that it is 5 to 20 times faster than the best alternative, requires less memory, and achieves similar accuracy. This illustrates the benefit of our symbolic GPU programming approach. Caspar is released as part of SymForce and is freely available at https://github.com/symforce-org/symforce

</details>


### [235] [ZAPS-DA: Zero-Phase Action Policy Smoothing with Decoupled Actor for Continuous Control in Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30612)
*Faiq Shamass*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 这篇论文提出了一种新框架ZAPS-DA，显著减少RL策略在物理执行中的动作抖动，无需后处理且无相位延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在实际物理环境中，离策略强化学习训练出的连续控制策略普遍存在高频动作抖动（jitter），直接用在物理执行器上不切实际。现有手段如后处理滤波虽然能减小抖动但引入延迟，结合平滑项进RL损失亦有副作用。针对以上实际问题亟需新的解决方案。

Method: ZAPS-DA框架包含两个策略网络：一个按常规方式训练（主actor），另一个解耦的actor则通过监督模仿回放缓冲区内经零相位滤波数据进行训练。最终实际部署时，仅用解耦actor，其为当前观测的前馈平滑输出，无需实时滤波，无需动作历史输入。这种方法本质上实现了'因果蒸馏'非因果滤波。所用损失函数无须调参，且可广泛适配不同优化器。

Result: 在MetaDrive和Webots自定义ACC环境中对比实验表明：ZAPS-DA可降低方向盘抖动14-21倍、油门抖动3-5倍且奖励损失仅为6.3%；在Webots环境中达到帕累托改进（同等奖励，8-45倍抖动降低，故障率从2%降到0.7%）。

Conclusion: ZAPS-DA为持续控制任务中减少动作抖动提供了高效且易部署的方法，不仅抖动显著降低，任务完成度基本无损，对实际物理系统具可推广性。

Abstract: Continuous control policies trained with off-policy reinforcement learning frequently exhibit high-frequency action jitter, rendering direct deployment on physical actuators impractical. Post-hoc filtering attenuates jitter but introduces phase lag; embedding smoothness penalties in the actor's loss couples them with the RL gradient and conflates reward regression with over-aggressive smoothing. We present ZAPS-DA, a framework that reduces action jitter at deployment with negligible phase lag and no post-processing. ZAPS-DA pairs an unmodified main actor (trained by the base RL loss) with a separate decoupled actor trained via supervised imitation of zero-phase filtered targets stored in the replay buffer. The deployed policy is the decoupled actor: a feed-forward map from the current observation to a smooth action, with no inference-time filter and no action-history input -- a mechanism we term causal distillation of a non-causal filter. A magnitude-matched MSE loss provides zero-hyperparameter portability across optimizer classes. Validated with Soft Actor-Critic and a Savitzky--Golay filter in two driving simulators using paired n=150 evaluation protocols: on MetaDrive, ZAPS-DA reduces steering jitter by 14--21x and throttle jitter by 3--5x (all $p < 10^{-4}$, Bonferroni-corrected) while matching task-completion (p=0.28 success, p=0.31 crash) at a 6.3% reward cost; on a custom Webots adaptive cruise control environment, the same SG configuration produces a Pareto improvement -- reward parity (p=0.121), 8--45x steering jitter reduction, and total task-failure rate reduced from 2.0% to 0.7%.

</details>


### [236] [Exploiting Chordal Sparsity for Globally Optimal Estimation with Factor Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30617)
*Avinash Subramanian,Connor Holmes,Timothy D. Barfoot,Frank Dellaert,Frederike Dümbgen*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在GTSAM框架内，自动化将任意常见因子和变量类型的因子图构建为凸SDP松弛的问题求解流程，并借助Bayes树分解大规模SDP问题，大幅提升在稀疏因子图上的求解效率。对比标准局部方法表现出优越的全局收敛和可扩展性。开源实现已提供。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器人感知、导航与控制高度依赖于稳健高效的状态估计。常规因子图求解器多为局部优化器，易陷入局部极值点，带来潜在安全风险；而基于凸松弛的全局方法，虽然安全但实现复杂且计算开销高。因此，急需一种兼具自动化、全局收敛性和高效性的状态估计方法。

Method: 作者在GTSAM软件包中提出自动构建针对常见因子和变量类型的SDP（半正定规划）松弛，并利用GTSAM的Bayes树结构，将大规模SDP分解成子问题，使其在稀疏（Chordally sparse）因子图下能大幅提升解算速度。

Result: 通过3D姿态图SLAM（环状因子图）和2D定位（链式因子图）两个案例，实验证明所提结构利用型全局估计器比标准局部求解器具有更优的扩展性（即计算复杂度随问题规摸增长缓慢）及全局收敛表现。

Conclusion: 该工作实现了状态估计问题凸松弛自动化与高效求解，克服了标准局部方法易陷入局部极值及凸松弛计算复杂度高的两大难题，显著提升了大规模状态估计问题的全局性与效率，对机器人领域具重要意义。

Abstract: Robust and efficient state estimation is crucial for perception, navigation, and control in robotics. State estimation problems are conveniently modeled using the factor-graph framework as enabled by modern software packages such as GTSAM or g2o. However, the standard solvers included in such frameworks are local and may converge to poor local minima, posing significant safety concerns. Conversely, techniques based on convex relaxations have been shown to provide a means of globally solving or certifying many state estimation problems. However, these relaxations 1) often require substantial effort to formulate, and 2) may incur significantly higher cost compared to efficient local solvers, as they require solving a large semidefinite program (SDP). In this work, we address both shortcomings by 1) creating a new procedure within the GTSAM framework for automatically constructing convex SDP relaxations for any factor graphs with common factor and variable types, and by 2) exploiting the Bayes tree constructions native to GTSAM to decompose the SDP problem, leading to significant speedup in solver time for chordally sparse problems. We demonstrate the favorable scaling of this structure-exploiting global estimator compared to standard local solvers for two case studies: A 3D pose-graph SLAM problem with a ring factor graph and a 2D localization problem with a chain factor graph. The software framework is available at https://github.com/borglab/gtsam.

</details>


### [237] [Bidirectional Incremental Generalized Hybrid A*](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30647)
*Sidharth Talia,Oren Salzman,Siddhartha Srinivasa*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文针对复杂动态系统在非结构化环境下的高效kinodynamic规划问题，提出了双向增量广义混合A*（Bi-IGHA*）算法，有效减少了搜索扩展次数且性能优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的A*和Hybrid A*在面对复杂系统和高维空间时计算效率低，而预生成运动基元在复杂环境下不可行。因此需要能高效、逐步改进的kinodynamic路径规划方法，并解决现有IGHA*因冻结顶点导致隐藏解的问题。

Method: 提出Bi-IGHA*方法，将IGHA*的单向逐层分辨率搜索扩展为双向搜索，以降低搜索深度并缓解冻结顶点隐藏有效解的现象。该方法保留了单向IGHA*的代价单调改进和终止性保证。

Result: 在R3、R4和R6等典型规划问题上，Bi-IGHA*显著减少了节点扩展次数。实验显示，在高速度无人越野自主行驶等实际kinodynamic规划应用中，Bi-IGHA*在保持闭环性能的同时大幅提高了搜索效率。

Conclusion: Bi-IGHA*在保持IGHA*优化和终止性质的前提下，进一步提升了对复杂动力学系统的规划效率，有望广泛应用于高难度自主运动规划任务。

Abstract: We focus on the problem of efficient anytime kinodynamic planning for systems with complex dynamics in unstructured environments that make precomputing motion primitives infeasible. Directly applying A* to such problems is computationally infeasible due to the curse of dimensionality. Methods such as Hybrid A* addressed this burden by discretizing the state space, but in turn creating a coupling between tree discovery and the discretization resolution. The Incremental Generalized Hybrid A* (IGHA*) performs search over a hierarchy of resolutions in an anytime fashion to break this coupling, by freezing vertices to use in later search iterations rather than pruning them. However, the frozen vertices can hide solution-supporting vertices from the search at a particular iteration. While classical bidirectional search is motivated by the reduction of search depth, extending IGHA* into the bidirectional setting (termed Bi-IGHA*) obtains additional benefit by fundamentally mitigating the behaviour induced by frozen vertices hiding solutions. We show that Bi-IGHA* preserves IGHA*'s guarantees on monotonic cost improvement and termination. We empirically show that Bi-IGHA* substantially reduces expansions on R3, R4, and R6 planning problems, and achieves equivalent closed-loop performance with kinodynamic planning for high-speed off-road autonomy while requiring significantly fewer expansions. Website: https://personalrobotics.github.io/IGHAStar/biighastar.html

### [238] [Primitive Subspaces Mediate Few-Shot Transfer in VLAs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30695)
*Anya Singh,Cabrel Happi,Jai Relan,Varun Nair,Vidyut Baradwaj*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文探索了通过增加对原始技能（primitive）的感知能力，提高视觉-语言-行动（VLA）模型在工业任务中低成本迁移新任务的效率，发现以primitive为中心的训练带来更高的few-shot学习效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前VLA模型在工业场景中迁移到新任务需要大量微调，成本高昂。为降低教学成本，作者希望探索能否通过原始技能的分解与组合，在无需微调的前提下实现高效任务迁移。

Method: 作者设计了两种VLA架构（OpenVLA与π_{0.5}），并在装配任务数据集（REASSEMBLE）上训练，分别采用平铺式整体轨迹和以primitive为单位分割的episode，并用对应的语言提示。持出未见过的任务和物体，评估通过极少数（few-shot）演示在无权重更新下的执行能力，比较两种训练方式的迁移表现。

Result: 以primitive为单位训练的模型仅需3条演示即能达到精调模型78%的性能，而平铺式训练方法需10条演示才能达到同等级别，表现出3倍的样本效率优势。对隐藏状态的primitive子空间消融会显著损害迁移效果，而消融随机子空间则无影响。

Conclusion: 以原始技能分解重组的方法极大提高了VLA在新任务上的few-shot迁移效率，并证实了primitive表示对于few-shot能力的因果关键作用。作者还指出了评估分段策略时必须注意的统计陷阱。

Abstract: Deploying vision-language-action (VLA) policies in industrial environments requires the ability to teach new tasks at low cost, a property current VLAs lack, since each new task requires fine-tuning. We investigate whether primitive-aware training produces a transferable artifact: a learned library of sub-skills that can be composed at inference time, conditioned on a small number of demonstrations, to perform tasks the policy was never trained on. We train two VLA architectures with different inductive biases, OpenVLA and $π_{0.5}$, on the REASSEMBLE contact-rich assembly dataset under matched LoRA fine-tuning recipes and locked hyperparameters, varying training between flat trajectories and primitive-segmented episodes with primitive-specific language prompts. We hold out 6 object-task combinations from training and evaluate few-shot transfer: models receive $m \in \{0, 1, 3, 5, 10\}$ demonstrations of a held-out task and attempt execution without weight updates. We replicate across three training seeds and validate on a second dataset (LIBERO-Long). Primitive-trained models reach 78% of fine-tuned upper-bound performance with only m=3 demonstrations, while flat-trained models require m=10 demonstrations to reach the same level -- a $3\times$ sample efficiency gap that replicates across seeds, architectures, and datasets. To establish causation, we ablate the primitive-decodable subspace of hidden states and show few-shot transfer degrades by 32 percentage points while ablating a random subspace of equal dimensionality has no effect, indicating primitive representations are causally necessary rather than incidentally correlated with transfer. We identify and correct a methodological pitfall in evaluating chunked policies: family-wise inflation of single-step action-range gates produces order-of-magnitude higher false-failure rates against ground-truth human demonstrations.

### [239] [Geometry-Aware Control Barrier Functions for Collision Avoidance via Bernstein Polynomial Approximations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30696)
*Siwon Jo,Yanze Zhang,Yupeng Yang,Wenhao Luo*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种基于Bernstein多项式有符号距离场（BP-SDFs）的几何感知控制障碍函数（CBF）新方法，实现对复杂几何形状下的机器人安全导航。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有CBF方法通常基于简单几何形状（如球体或超椭球体）来近似机器人和障碍物，这在非结构化环境下或遇到不规则物体时易显得过于保守，或需大量局部近似体，导致实时性能下降。因此，亟需一种能统一、精确表达不规则形状并便于实施安全控制的新方法。

Method: 提出用Bernstein多项式有符号距离场（BP-SDFs）统一表达机器人与障碍物的几何，并基于此设计能刻画最小安全距离的新型CBF。借助BP-SDFs的可微性，方便将CBF控制约束嵌入闭环控制系统。

Result: 通过仿真实验证明：该方法在不同环境下，无论单机器人还是异构多机器人避碰任务中，均能有效提升安全性，并兼具较高的实时性。

Conclusion: BP-SDFs驱动的几何感知CBF为复杂场景下机器人安全导航提供了高效统一的解决方案，相比传统方法更灵活且能提升导航安全和系统响应效率。

Abstract: Safe navigation often relies on well-defined conditions based on the shape of robots and obstacles, and can be challenging when they have irregular geometries. While Control Barrier Functions (CBFs) offer an efficient mechanism to enforce safe set forward invariance, common shape surrogates (e.g., spheres or super-ellipsoids) either are overly conservative in unstructured scenes or require many local primitives, which inflates constraint counts and degrades real-time performance. In this paper, we introduce a novel geometry-aware Control Barrier Function (CBF) based on Bernstein-Polynomial Signed Distance Fields (BP-SDFs). It provides a unified way to represent the obstacles and robots, so as to represent the barrier function with a unified minimum distance. Benefiting from the differentiability of the Bernstein polynomials, one can easily enforce the control constraints in a closed loop. We validate the method's efficiency and performance to guarantee safety in single-robot navigation and heterogeneous multi-robot collision avoidance via simulations under different environments.

### [240] [GSAM: A Generalizable and Safe Robotic Framework for Articulated Object Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30740)
*Beichen Shao,Mengying Xie,Heng Su,Wanyi Zhang,Mingyan Li,Yan Ding,Fausto Giunchiglia,Chao Chen*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了GSAM框架，通过融合视觉感知、VLM推理和LLM驱动的约束生成，实现了服务机器人对多样关节物体的安全、高效操控，且显著提升了泛化能力和安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前机器人操控关节类物体时，现有方法往往忽略物体差异性和末端执行器与手柄之间复杂交互，导致泛化能力弱和操作中的破坏性碰撞问题。因此亟需一种兼具更好泛化性和交互安全性的解决方案。

Method: GSAM框架包括四个主要环节：1）以视觉感知器预测物体运动学参数；2）通过微调后的VLM和链式思维（CoT）推理校正感知输出，增强常识推理能力；3）设计交互约束生成器，将目标物、交互位姿和避障知识内化为通用约束模板，并通过LLM函数化约束应用于轨迹与姿态规划；4）运动学感知操控规划器对规划结果进行可达性验证。

Result: 在5类关节物体、50组铰链任务及50组随机末端执行器-手柄初始配置下测试，GSAM框架使操作成功率较最佳基线提升36%，标准差下降3.1%，显著体现了在复杂实际场景下的泛化与安全优势。

Conclusion: GSAM证明了结合多模态感知、常识推理与运动学约束的方法在提升机器人操控关节物体的通用性和安全性上的有效性，对服务机器人实际应用有重要意义。

Abstract: Articulated object manipulation is a unique challenge for service robots. Existing methods employ end-to-end policy learning, visionmotion planning, and large-language/visual-language model (LLM/VLM), but often overlook the diversity of articulated objects and the complexity of interactions between end-effector and handle, leading to limited generalization and destructive collisions. To address this, we propose GSAM, a generalizable and safe robotic framework for articulated object manipulation. Specifically, a vision-based perceiver generates the kinematic parameters. Considering that pre-trained markers in perceiver yield raw estimations that may deviate from commonsense, we present a f ine-tuned VLM-based refiner, using chain-of-thought (COT) commonsense reasoning to refine perception. To prevent destructive collisions, we design an interaction constraint function generator, integrating articulated object, interaction pose, and obstacle avoidance knowledge into a base. LLM then functionalize these constraints and apply them to trajectory and posture planning. A kinematic-aware manipulation planner verifies reachability for trajectory and posture. Experiments on 50 hinge tasks across 5 object categories and 50 randomly initialized end-effectorhandle configurations show that GSAM reduces standard deviation by 3.1% and improves manipulation success rate by 36.0% compared to the best baseline, respectively demonstrating the superior object generalization and interaction safety of GSAM in practical scenarios.

</details>

Abstract: Extending humanoid traversal to the open world is key to practical deployment in human environments, but remains challenging. The robot must use vision to ensure safe and reliable foot placement on heterogeneous terrain under highly dynamic motion, while producing coordinated, natural whole-body behaviors. We propose SSR, an efficient end-to-end framework for egocentric vision-based humanoid traversal that jointly learns these capabilities. SSR introduces imagined foothold guidance, which learns to model forthcoming swing-foot contacts and evaluates their support to guide pre-touchdown swings toward stable regions, reducing edge slips. It further employs equivariant latent-space symmetry augmentation to efficiently induce bilateral coordination under high-dimensional visual observations, and uses terrain-specific multi-discriminator motion priors to encourage human-like behavior across scenes. Extensive experiments show that SSR achieves safe, stable, and high-quality locomotion on diverse real-world terrains, including stairs with varied structures and extreme challenges such as wide gaps and high platforms, while enabling reliable long-horizon traversal in open outdoor environments.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先，作者把真实问题简化为仅对目标物体的规划，假设物体可被直接控制。然后将得到的物体轨迹用于后续机器人-物体联合规划的问题，形成分层规划。该方法使用MPPI控制框架，将物体的轨迹作为参考以引导机器人的动作。

Result: 该方法在模拟和实际的6自由度机械臂推物实验中进行了验证。与常规MPPI相比，分层MPPI在模拟中成功率提升40%，控制频率提升26%；在实际实验中，成功率提升20%，计算量基本不变。

Abstract: Long-horizon planning for non-prehensile robot manipulation is challenging due to underactuated and discontinuous interactions. We first solve a simplified object-only problem, assuming the object can be actuated directly, and use the planned object trajectory as a reference in solving the joint robot-object planning problem. We evaluate our method in both simulation and hardware using a 6-DoF xArm6 manipulator to perform object pushing tasks in which the target object must reach a goal while avoiding static obstacles, necessitating non-myopic reasoning. Our object-informed MPPI increases task success by 40\% with a 26\% faster control frequency in simulation, and by 20\% in real experiments with similar computation as regular MPPI.

We show analytically how two vibratory waveform parameters, the sticking acceleration and the slipping acceleration, affect average part velocity when moving against gravity. The theoretical trends are then validated using an experimental setup where the squeeze force is controlled and part motion is recorded by a high-resolution encoder. We also develop a 2-DoF vibratory surface capable of translation in one direction and rotation about the surface normal. Using two of these 2-DoF surfaces in a parallel jaw gripper configuration, we bidirectionally translate and rotate a variety of grasped parts, as well as demonstrate that the same waveform trends for translation also persist for in-plane rotation.

Method: 提出Feat2Go框架，由预训练视觉世界模型提取进展目标，通过分割语义阶段与趋势聚类实现补充监督信号，进而训练价值模型来预测阶段性进展，并在策略优化中利用该价值重塑终端奖励，无需手工奖励设计。兼容主流RL算法如PPO、GRPO。
